                      <div data-reactid="701">
                       Bright &amp; spacious private room with a Queen bed close to many studios such as Warner Bros, Nickelodeon, Disney, and NBCUniversal.                       </div>
                      <div data-reactid="702">
                       Our private bedroom is bright, spacious and quiet. Located on the 2nd floor of our Townhouse in safe and residential Burbank, it receives light throughout the day. The room features a Queen bed which can comfortably accommodate two people. The bed can fold into a comfortable 3-seater sofa giving a lot of space to the room. There is also a bedside table and reading light, floor-to-ceiling mirrors, a large closet for your clothes and belongings, a lock on the door and complete shut out blinds. There is also storage space for your bags. Our townhouse is a true oasis of calm, and well connected to Los Angeles and the San Fernando Valley. We're housed in a block of Townhouses, and being at the very front facing the street we have some lovely views of the mountains and the valley, as well as receiving light in all areas of the house. The Townhouse is modern and comfortable, with wooden floors on the first floor and carpet on the second floor. When you're staying here it's hard to believe you are just a few miles away from all the major studios and shopping and entertainment options available.
                      </div>
                      <div data-reactid="703">
                       We live on a safe, quiet, palm-tree lined residential street in Burbank, near many of the major studios. These and several fantastic shopping and entertainment centers are very close to us, either via car or public transport: Burbank Town Center (Mall/Cinema/Dining) - 1 mile Nickelodeon Studios - 1.2 miles Disney Studios - 2.1 miles Warner Brothers - 3.1 miles Glendale Galleria (Mall/Dining) - 3 miles The Americana (Mall/Cinema/Dining) - 3 miles NBC/Universal Studios - 4.3 miles Hollywood Walk of Fame - 5.4 miles away We're walking distance to a Smart &amp; Final Extra, several coffee shops including Starbucks, fast food places such as Taco Bell, Del Taco, McDonalds &amp; Habit Burger, and there is a great Japanese sushi place a couple of minutes away called Momotoro. We're also close to a CVS and Trader Joe's. It's a 20 minute drive to Hollywood, or just 15 to Griffith Park &amp; Observatory - either is a great place to see the Hollywood sign, and we can give you a lot of recommendations on sights to see, hikes to go on, things to do and places to go. There is great nightlife in North and West Hollywood, both a short drive away.
